This is a new fragrance. <b>MYSLF Le Parfum</b> was launched in 2024. MYSLF Le Parfum was created by Daniela Andrier, Antoine Maisondieu and Christophe Raynaud. Top note is Black Pepper; middle note is Orange Blossom; base notes are Bourbon Vanilla, Amber, Patchouli and Woody Notes. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>MYSLF Le Parfum is a more intense interpretation of the men's fragrance "MYSLF Eau de Parfum." This new version has evolved to offer a deeper and more powerful experience. The signature blend of soft orange blossom and textured wood in MYSLF is enhanced by spicy black pepper and sweet vanilla bourbon, culminating in a sensual amber finish.</p>

<p>The packaging features a black color scheme and a slender silhouette, capturing the essence of YSL. The glossy "Cassandra logo" is prominently displayed on the bold matte black glass, creating a design that is both powerful and sophisticated.</p>

<br />
I'm not sure what they're trying to do. It's too feminine for a male scent, and too indecisive to be a unisex scent. This smells like a non-binary sibling of Libre.<br />
<br />
The vanilla and orange blossom is too thick to be enjoyed in any other season other than winter. I can't see any masculine male wearing on a formal or informal outfit -- and mind you, I own Toy Boy. I just don't know what the hell they're trying to achieve. <br />
<br />
The performance is alright, though.<br />
<br />
Hard pass.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2330847"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2330847#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2330749" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2330749"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2330749#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2329075" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2329075" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tracershy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1181886"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="tracershy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Azzaro/The-Most-Wanted-66826.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.66826.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Most Wanted"title="The Most Wanted"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2329075ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2329075" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1181886">tracershy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-27">10/27/24 06:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Le Parfum is definitely better than its predecessor released last year, which, to put it mildly, was embarrassingly weak and I'm not surprised that it was met with such a wave of criticism.<br />
The new YSL perfumes have primarily got rid of the vulgarly artificial shampoo note known from the classic edition. These were poor synthetics straight from the cheapest perfumes, associated with the artificial freshness of a spray deodorant or with the scent of a shampoo from the lowest shelf. Fortunately, this is not here.<br />
Although there is still no delight, I must admit that at times it came out even interestingly, especially in the opening.<br />
First of all, the orange blossom is emphasized here in a way similar to the male classics from years ago, when creators were not afraid to place this intoxicating flower in the center of the composition in men's perfumes. Of course, it is very far from the iconic JPG Fleur Du Male, but when smelling the new MYSLF, memories of that perfume sometimes awaken.  Vanilla has been added to the white flowers, which sweetens the composition a lot, but so that it is not too feminine, woody notes have been added, and a bit of pepper to start with. However, the perfume is still very close to Libre Intense, which I perceive as a feminine scent and which, to be honest, I do not like. In MYSLF Le Parfum, it is even less rough than in Libre. Thanks to the vanilla, the orange blossom becomes sweeter in an almost syrupy way. There is also no greater depth in this composition.<br />
I still perceive this perfume as a more feminine perfume, unisex at best. At times it is not bad, I put it much higher than its predecessor, but it is still an average level and it is far from the top premieres of 2024. In addition, when the scent sits on the skin for a while, I start to have associations with a very confident older lady in a fur coat, which is irritating.<br />
The parameters for the concentration of the perfume are average.  Longevity is about 5-6 hours, projection is clear shortly after application, but it fades away quite quickly and sticks delicately to the skin. Overall, the whole thing is average. Especially when you look at the price of this perfume.<br />
<br />
5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2329075"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2329075#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2328665" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2328665" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ben&amp;Jerry"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2074821"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2074821.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ben&amp;Jerry" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Eau-de-Parfum-84094.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.84094.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="MYSLF Eau de Parfum"title="MYSLF Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2328665ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2328665" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2074821">Ben&amp;Jerry</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-26">10/26/24 16:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not my cup of tea… while I do love the OG for its citric and sharp presentation of the Orange blossom this one just comes off as “just another- Rabanne” fragrance to my nose. I find it interesting that so few people actually have drawn the parallels to Rabanne… to me it could easily have been “One million” when smelled up front. As for the composition: it’s way too spicy and vanilla forward for my taste. It actually drowns the orange blossom completely from the scent profile in my opinion. Mind you, When I complain about the vanilla accord in this fragrance it’s mainly because it’s a dirty vanilla and not a warm, creamy vanilla, cause that I could dig. <br />
<br />
As for those of you who claim that this fragrance is redundant to own due to its supposed similarity to the OG I couldn’t disagree more. It’s very different and, to my nose, inferior to the original. <br />
Summed up I’ll cherish the OG some more, but won’t jump on the Le Parfum wagon. <br />
<br />
Scent: 3/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10 (Good, but not excellent)<br />
Sillage: 7/10<br />
Gender: male- more so than the OG <br />
Value for money: 4/10<br />
Versatility: 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2328665"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2328665#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2326640" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

Smells good, but there's not much depth, just another "dumb reach" fragrance on the market.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2300188"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2300188#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2300137" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1301200">TheMicRuler</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-29">09/29/24 17:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I tested this on skin at a local Sephora, and found it pleasant. It's slightly sweet, aromatic, and ambery. In the dry down, there is some nuance that I rather enjoy; probably the patchouli note. Deep into the dry down all I really smell is the vanilla. Performance was better than expected - I could catch wafts for the first couple hours.<br />
<br />
This is a solid fragrance for someone who is just starting their collection and looking for a mass appealing winter time scent to wear as a daily driver. In that context, it's a reasonably safe blind buy, particularly from discounters.<br />
<br />
If you've got a large collection (10+ bottles), you probably already have something that fits that role and shouldn't blind buy this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Definitely a unisex scent. It smells designer and "perfumey" but strikes a nice androgynous balance between a citrus-woody "bro" scent and a more feminine vanilla-amber-citrus-patchouli scent. It does smell like a couple that wears mall fragrances, but in a perfectly pleasant way. Not everything has to be a super unique niche scent. I like it and if I smelled it on someone I'd think they'd smell nice. I'll pass it onto someone else but it's better than I expected.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2292858"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2292858#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289914" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2253618" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="superfish0012"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2090623"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="superfish0012" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-2318.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.2318.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Versace Pour Homme"title="Versace Pour Homme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2253618ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2253618" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2090623">superfish0012</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-18">08/18/24 18:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really quite like MYSLF Le Parfum. Granted, it was given to me for free by a friend who works in the beauty industry and is absolutely inundated with product familiarization freebies.<br />
<br />
The smell is great, first off. Black pepper on top very quickly (and I mean within ten minutes) fades away leaving a lovely, almost orange creamsicle like orange-vanilla with white floral notes. The wood is also noticeable and rounds it out well. <br />
<br />
It lasts close to the skin for about 8 hours or so, in my experience (moderate temperature, indoors).<br />
<br />
Oddly, it seems to either have a rather long-lasting-but-subtle sillage, or doesn't have any trail at all, and it just depends on the person smelling it, I guess? For context, one friend who is rather sensitive to scents of all sorts didn't notice it at all until he was close enough to kiss me, and another could smell it in a room I'd left five minutes prior rather clearly. <br />
<br />
It's a very beautiful, gentle smell. Some other users have said it's very feminine but I disagree. It's masculine but just not in a "beard and flannel" type of way.<br />
<br />
It's also incredibly versatile. I'll say it leans wintery and evening, but only because I've got more obviously summery fragrances in my collection and it's got a certain intimacy to it. An excellent date night fragrance, I'll say.<br />
<br />
Overall, I highly recommend MYSLF Le Parfum.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2253618"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2253618#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2253344" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I kept smelling my hand where I sprayed it afterwards, and I enjoyed talking to the lady at the store about fragrances, so I went back on Sunday and bought a little bottle of it.<br />
<br />
I just used it for a full spraying this morning.  I used five or six sprays from the refillable 10 ml bottle, so I think those sprays are less voluminous than a full size bottle, but it seems like I can still smell it about an hour and a half later.  It reminds me a lot of Azzaro The Most Wanted Parfum.  I have a small bottle of Libre L'absolu Platine too; I just saw that other people say it smells like that, so I will definitely compare them myself, or myslf? ;-)<br />
<br />
I'm really enjoying this fragrance so far.  I couldn't begin to describe the specific aromas, but they agree with my nose very well.  I think I paid about $40 with tax, so that's about the going rate for 10 ml travel sprays.  I get that you have to pay more by volume for a smaller amount.  I might buy a bigger bottle; I'm not sure.  It seems like YSL fragrances are on the expensive side.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2247640"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2247640#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2246340" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1477503">Siprian85</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-03">08/03/24 17:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Fragrance Notes:<br />
<br />
Top Notes:<br />
Black Pepper.<br />
<br />
Mid Notes:<br />
Orange Blossom.<br />
<br />
Base Notes:<br />
Bourbon Vanilla, Patchouli, Amber, Woody Notes.<br />
 Fragrance Review: <br />
<br />
First thoughts, this is a sharper/Intense version of Myslf Le Parfum. <br />
<br />
- It starts off very similar with a warm spicy white floral scent, and Amber in the drydown. <br />
<br />
- I sprayed a total of 5 times. Twice behind each ear, twice on the front of neck, and once in front of my chest. The longevity is good, it lasts approximately 6 hours on my skin, projects for about an arms length for 30 minutes to 1 hour before turning into a skin scent. It does however lasts a few days on my clothes.<br />
 (Depends on skin types)<br />
<br />
Overall Rating  (7/10)<br />
Very similar to the EDP, however, it's much more feminine in my honest opinion, where the white floral notes and Vanilla is much more intense with a hint of spicyness. It's a great smelling scent, but can be redundant if you already own the EDP.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2238047"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2238047#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2237892" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is easily better to my nose than the eau de parfum -- not to mention much less feminine. The original had a fuzzy, starchy laundry smell to it. This is a much more grounded, somewhat earthy white floral that veers in the direction of many feminine fragrance profiles but arrests itself squarely back into traditionally masculine territory with a dark creamy woodiness. <br />
<br />
I won't wear the eau de parfum because I don't want to smell like fabric softener - or have to live with that caustic, suffocating cloud that some white florals give off. I will wear this because it does not veer into that territory and is unique from others in my collection due to the primacy of the orange blossom. <br />
<br />
And no it absolutely is not like the most wanted line lol.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2237892"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2237892#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2236998" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It's softer, warmer, and more rounded, it's more of an evening scent which I think really suits this DNA.<br />
<br />
It's nothing groundbreaking but it simply works, it's easygoing, smells extremely pleasant and performs extremely well. <br />
If you already have a large, varied collection and are looking for more niche stuff, then this isn't for you, but if you want an inoffensive, casual designer  scent for moderate climates then this is definitely above average.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2231947" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DarthFragrance"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1639884"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1639884.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DarthFragrance" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Superleggera-95753.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.95753.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Allure Homme Sport Superleggera"title="Allure Homme Sport Superleggera"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2231947ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2231947" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1639884">DarthFragrance</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-28">07/28/24 12:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just blind bought a 100mL of this. I've been really digging YSL fragrances lately and I really like MYSLF EDP so I figured this was a safe blind buy. My first immediate observation was that this is much fresher than I was expecting. It's not dark at all, it's a fresh fragrance. Think spring, fall and summer nights. It's a proper flanker in the sense that the similarities to MYSLF EDP are apparent with that core DNA. For that reason, I think the best way to describe MYSLF Le Parfum is to compare and contrast it to the EDP. <br />
<br />
Orange blossom is in both the EDP and Le Parfum but plays a more prominent role in Le Parfum. Think of it like removing all the citrus that the EDP had and replacing it with more orange blossom. This makes Le Parfum even more unisex than the EDP, which is also unisex but leans more masculine in comparison. The generous dose of black pepper in Le Parfum keeps it from straying too feminine and keeps it decidedly unisex. The other most notable change is the removal of ambrofix in Le Parfum because ambrofix has very distinctive characteristics, primarily the musk accords it provides in the EDP. There's also something aldehydic in the Le Parfum, distinctly reminiscent of the aldehydes used in YSL Y Le Parfum. The most surprising part of Le Parfum is how fresh the base notes are, that's what I was totally not expecting. The amber, vanilla, woods and patchouli are unusually fresh.<br />
<br />
As for performance, Le Parfum is long lasting but has soft projection. The EDP has better performance, lasting a little bit longer and projecting noticeably more. Le Parfum doesn't have bad performance, the EDP just performs noticeably better on me. <br />
<br />
Overall, I like the EDP a bit more as of now. I like the balance of bergamot and orange blossom more than just a huge dose of orange blossom. I prefer the base notes in the EDP of ambrofix and patchouli because I am addicted to the musk accords the ambrofix provides, I love it. I also like the EDP's better performance. That said, YSL makes amazing fragrances and is a top designer brand. I blind bought Le Parfum for a reason and I'm not disappointed. It smells high quality, versatile and has a classiness about it. It smells like a YSL fragrance, which is a good thing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2231947"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2231947#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231711" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Any time any place any season !!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2223177"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2223177#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222806" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2222806" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="FragrancyHobby"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1174325"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1174325.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="FragrancyHobby" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2222806ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2222806" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1174325">FragrancyHobby</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-18">07/18/24 18:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I sure am glad I've gotten used to ordering samples/decants before buying anything new! While I still enjoy the anticipation of a new release that captures my attention, I have to say it's been quite a few years now since I've purchased a bottle of a new release. In fact, my last purchase of a new bottle was Chanel Allure Homme Sport. Prior to that, I want to say it was Dior Sauvage back in the summer that it was released. At first, I thought it was just me, but as I read more reviews of recent releases, the once-was enthusiasm for at least a FEW new fragrances a year seems to have diminished. I'm left feeling robbed of the hobby I once enjoyed so very much by the way these companies are releasing subpar s**t!<br />
<br />
With the initial MYSLF release last year, I was left disappointed. I remember EXACTLY where I was when I first tested it. At the time, I couldn't recall WHAT it reminded me of, but many months later it came to me. There's a cheap/plastic-like note that's found in Estee Lauder Pleasures for Men. Given the dark bottle, the really creative name, etc., I guess I let MYSLF (errr, myself) get too carried away with anticipation of something good.<br />
<br />
So here we are a year later and I have to ask MYSLF once again... WHY?!<br />
<br />
My sample of MYSLF Le Parfum arrived today and what a train wreck! Oddly, the VERY, and I mean VERY first thing that came to mind was an aftershave/cologne my dad used to wear back in the day when I was a kid called Blue Stratos, which was released in 1974. While I have good memories of seeing that on the shelf in the bathroom and dad wearing it to special events, etc., it did not make an impression on me today. I was REALLY looking forward to a darker MYSLF with the vanilla and patchouli, but this is essentially the same as the original, just on steroids. Nothing new, nothing to get excited about and CERTAINLY not worthy of the price! I smell zero patchouli or vanilla in this at all. Speaking of that, I'm really getting tired of fragrance pyramids not living up to their claims, but that's a different topic for another time.<br />
<br />
One other observation I've noticed after about 30-45 minutes with MYSLF Le Parfum, it dries down into something that smells like the interior of a junk/trinket store. It's not a smell of candles or anything like some of those stores can smell like, but just a very plastic/cheap knick-knacks smell with some fruity old candy mixed in.<br />
<br />
Truly revolting, and with the price point, absolutely insulting!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2222806"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2222806#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222555" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2222555" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Olere Novum"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1949919"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1949919.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Olere Novum" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Scents-of-Wood/Praline-in-Maple-75894.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.75894.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Praline in Maple"title="Praline in Maple"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2222555ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2222555" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1949919">Olere Novum</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-18">07/18/24 12:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I received my bottle today from Ulta at 20% off the retail price if you have a healthy account with Ulta. Other account levels are 10% or 15% off for the next few days, depending on how much you have bought from Ulta in the past. Even a brand new account is 10% off right now.<br />
<br />
I was hesitant to buy this, especially without having the patience to wait and get it down the road through a discounter at 50% off retail, and particularly because so many people have said it is somewhat similar to the original. I find it to be extremely different from the OG. The white floral / orange blossom accord is extremely strong ... almost cloying. It is much smoother, softer and slightly less masculine to me than the original. I like it, and I definitely do not think you should avoid getting it because you have heard it is similar to the original and therefore redundant. They are different.<br />
<br />
The Le Parfum also has a muted bubblegum sweetness to it ... like what 30 year old guys that were raised on One Million, Invictus and Ultra Male have graduated to. It is not really immature or youthful smelling, just a bit too sweet for my liking - kind of like YSL Y EDP.  That has too much apple, and this has too much orange blossom and vanilla. I also agree 100% with the comparisons made to Gucci Guilty Elixir and the Libre line.<br />
<br />
All in all it is good but not great. It certainly does not hold a candle to Dior Sauvage Elixir, Bleu de Chanel Parfum, or JPG Le Male Elixir. And I would caution you not to blind buy this. Have more patience than I did and wait until you can smell a tester at the mall or get a sample because it smells more like it should be an Invictus or One Million Parfum than a Myslf Parfum to my nose.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2222555"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2222555#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222370" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2222370" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="maxpowerboston"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1089734"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1089734.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="maxpowerboston" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2222370ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2222370" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1089734">maxpowerboston</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-18">07/18/24 09:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've only smelled the original MYSLF on a test strip at Ulta once. I dismissed it as a pretty lame scent that smelled a lot like most other new, sweet, amberwood scents released since 2015 or so. I ended up getting a free bottle of MYSLF Le Parfum to test, so I wore it for three days in a row. It had an immediate similarity to what I recall the first scent smelling like but with a bunch of florals and a deep vanilla base. It has that same core that's in stuff like Polo 67 or Invictus or Phantom: a sweet woody thing. This one just has a lot of floral and vanilla added to it. It doesn't really smell feminine because of that amberwood core thing that is so common to young male mall releases today, but the florals were a bit surprising. There's a spiciness that I can smell in the mid (that sort of disappears by the dry down) that adds some interest.<br />
<br />
Longevity is pretty strong in my 3 wearings at 7-9 hours but projection was soft after 30 minutes. Sillage was noticeable still after 3-4 hours while I moved around but it wasn't what I'd call strong.<br />
<br />
A 7.0/10 for me. It's not bad but I'd not go out of my way to get this. Decent for cool weather date nights for younger men, I'd say.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2222370"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2222370#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2221581" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
$180.00 for 3.4<br />
150.00 for 1.7<br />
<br />
Outrageous!<br />
<br />
<br />
Now on to the scent.<br />
<br />
This is a more mature version of the original. I've been wearing it for a couple of hours now and at first you get a nice pepper opening which segues  into the original blossom note from the original. That mid melds with a nice vanilla and woodsy dry down. But to be completely honest, this reminds me of a mint free Le Male. This could have been it's own fragrance and not a flanker of Myslf. The original is far more superior and to be honest more creative than this. Definitely not worth the process they asking for it. Stick with the original.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2202990"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2202990#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202692" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1445544">jbozz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 23:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Just picked this up at a Macy’s in the Los Angeles area (it doesn’t officially launch until mid-to-late July) and it is super nice. The Le Parfum flanker is a slightly darker, spicier and a mildy sweeter take on the original MYSLF, and this feels more geared towards date night and evenings out on the town. There’s an added refinement and a luxury soapiness to it that I really, really enjoy. The added pepper and vanilla notes are present but they are blended so well here that they perfectly complement the rest of the composition and don’t overpower anything. This doesn’t really remind me of anything else except the original EDP so those making comparisons to Valentino Born in Roma Intense or a Layton exclusif clone are way off. Even though its more evening oriented it still has that freshness which makes it versatile enough for daytime use as well. All in all, if you’re a fan of the original release (which honestly is a great all around fragrance no matter what anybody says) then you’ll quite enjoy having this one too for more formal and intimate occasions. And the matte black bottle is just sexy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2202679"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2202679#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202504" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I've tried a bunch of other YSL after I got the MYSLF eau de Parfum and would say it's the best. This is decent too but the original is better. So one thing to note is that there's no citrus in this. So don't listen to reviewers saying it's like the original.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="94983"comment_id="2277482"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/MYSLF-Le-Parfum-94983.html?ccid=2277482#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2253344" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
